#include<stdio.h>
#include<string.h>
int anag(char [] , char []);
void main()
{
    char s1[100],s2[100];
    printf("\t\t\t*****INPUT*****\n");
    printf("Enter the strings");
    gets(s1);
    gets(s2);
    printf("\t\t\t*****OUTPUT*****\n");
    if(anag(s1,s2))
      {
         printf("Anagram");
      }
     else
        printf("Not Anagram");

}
int anag(char  s1[], char s2[])
{
    int l1=strlen(s1);
    int l2=strlen(s2);
    int f[26]={0};
    for(int i=0;i<l1;i++)
    {
        f[s1[i]-97]++;
    }
    for(int i=0;i<l2;i++)
    {
        f[s2[i]-97]--;
    }
    for(int i=0;i<26;i++)
    {
        if(f[i]!=0)
            return 0;
    }
    return 1;
}

int rev(int *p)
{
    int n=0;
    while(*p!=0)
    {
        n=(n*10)+((*p)%10);
        *p=*p/10;
    }
    return n;
}

Hello Everyone!

We, *The Designnovation Hub*, in collaboration with *ACM AND ACM-W* are excited to announce an upcoming interactive session *“MENTOR MIX”* where you can learn from the experiences and insights of some high-achieving 3rd and 4th year *students having an experience* in companies like *ATLASSIAN, MICROSOFT, ADOBE, AMAZON, ZSCALER, FLIPKART, LINKEDIN, and have done research at IIIT delhi.*

The session will be an open forum where you can engage in a dialogue with some of the most successful students in our program. They will share their insights on *topics* such as: 
✅Placement preparations and extracurriculars
✅Different projects and technical skills
✅Resume building
✅Online assessments
✅Research and academia
✅Application processes
✅Cold emailing
✅Pursuing masters abroad
✅Time Management
✅Navigating social life along with academics

The event aims at providing students of the first and second year with some tips. The learnings of the speakers would help the audience prepare in the best way for their careers with the proper guidance and support. 

Whether you are just starting out or have been studying for a while, you are sure to benefit from this session.

Please mark your calendars for the event, which will take place on 📆*8th April 2023* at ⏰*2 PM onwards* and *do register yourself!*
🏫Venue for the event: *Seminar hall; CSIT Block*

📜*Certificate of attendance will be provided*

Registration link: https://forms.gle/SB8q97o6p9Sq1MVd8

🍀Also, give a follow to TDH’s instagram page: @tdhgeu 

_We look forward to seeing you there! 🌻_

The film follows Peter Quill, a human thief who becomes the target of a manhunt after stealing a mysterious orb. Quill forms an uneasy alliance with a group of misfits: Gamora, a green-skinned assassin; Drax the Destroyer, a vengeful warrior; Rocket, a genetically-engineered raccoon; and Groot, a sentient tree-like creature. Together, they must stop Ronan the Accuser, a powerful alien villain who seeks to use the orb to destroy an entire planet. The team eventually discovers that the orb is actually an Infinity Stone, one of six immensely powerful artifacts that could grant ultimate power to anyone who possesses them. With the help of the Nova Corps, a space police force, the Guardians defeat Ronan and save the galaxy. In the end, they decide to stay together as a team, setting the stage for future adventures.

5/17/23, 08:43 - Satwik Geu: #include<stdio.h>
struct emp
{
	char name[10];
	int id;
	char address[100];
};
void main()
{
	int  n;
	printf("\t\t\t*****INPUT*****\n");
	printf("Enter the number of student\n");
	scanf("%d",&n);
	struct emp a[5];
	for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
	{
		printf("Enter the name of student, id and address\n");
		scanf(" %s",a[i].name);
		scanf("%d",&a[i].id);
		scanf(" %s",a[i].address);
	}
	
	struct emp temp;
	for(int i=0;i<n-1;i++)
	{
		for(int j=i+1;j<n;j++)
		{
			if(a[i].name[0]>a[j].name[0])
			{
				temp=a[i];
				a[i]=a[j];
				a[j]=temp;
			}
		}
	}
	printf("\t\t\t***OUTPUT***\n");
	for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
	{
		
		printf(" %s",a[i].name);
		printf("%d",a[i].id);
		printf(" %s",a[i].address);
		printf("\n");  
	}
	
		
	
}

struct student
{
  char name[40];
  int roll;
  char dep[20];
  char course[20];
  int yr;
 };
 void year(struct student s[],int n)
 {
   int i,y;
   printf("Input a particular year\n");
   scanf("%d",&y);
   for(i=0;i<n;i++)
   {
    if(s[i].yr==y)
    {
      printf("OUTPUT\n");
      printf("name is %s\n",s[i].name);
     }
    }
   }
   void rollnumber(struct student s[],int n)
   {
     int r,i;
     printf("OUTPUT\n")
     printf("Input roll number\n");
     scanf("%d",&r);
     for(i=0;i<n;i++)
     {
       if(s[i].roll==r)
       {
        printf("%s %s %s \n",s[i].name,s[i].dep,s[i].course);
        printf("%d\n",s[i].roll);
        printf("%d\n",s[i].yr);
        }
      }
     }
     
 void main()
 {
  int n=3;
  struct student s[n];
  int i;
  printf("Enter details of student:name,department,course,roll number,year of joining\n");
  for(i=0;i<n;i++)
  {
    scanf("%s %s %s ",s[i].name,s[i].dep,s[i].course);
    scanf("%d",&s[i].roll);
    scanf("%d",&s[i].yr);
   }
   year(s,n);
   rollnumber(s,n);
  }

int isprime(int num)
{
  for(int i=2;i<num;i++)
   {
     if(num%i==0)
      return 0;
    }
 return 1;
}

void main()
{
 FILE *fp,*p,*np;
 fp=fopen("Input.txt","w+");
 p=fopen("Prime.txt","w+");
 np=fopen("Non_prime.txt","w+");
 int num,i,c=0;
 printf("\t\t\t\tINPUT\n");
 for(i=0;i<20;i++)
 {
   scanf("%d",&num);
   putw(num,fp);
 }
   rewind(fp);
   while((num=getw(fp))!=EOF)
    {
      if(isprime(num))
	{
	  putw(num,p);
	}
       else
	{
	  putw(num,np);
	}
     }
    fclose(fp);
    rewind(np);
    rewind(p);
    printf("Prime numbers are:");
    while((num=getw(p))!=EOF)
     {
        printf(" %d",num);
      }
    printf("\nNon prime numbers are:");
    while((num=getw(np))!=EOF)
     {
        printf(" %d",num);
      }
     fclose(p);
     fclose(np);
}

9/5/23, 12:38 - Satwik Geu: #include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

int main() {
    char input[100];
    printf("Enter a multi-word string: ");
    fgets(input, sizeof(input), stdin);

    char *token = strtok(input, " "); // Tokenize the input string using space as the delimiter

    while (token != NULL) {
        printf("Length of '%s' is %zu\n", token, strlen(token));
        token = strtok(NULL, " "); // Get the next token
    }

    return 0;
}
9/5/23, 12:38 - Satwik Geu: This program first reads the multi-word string using fgets, then tokenizes it using strtok, and calculates the length of each word using strlen. It continues to tokenize and print the length of words until there are no more words left in the input string.

/*              !!!NOTE CAREFULLY THE REVERSAL CONDITION!!!                       */



class Solution {
    public ListNode addTwoNumbers(ListNode l1, ListNode l2) {
        //step 1 :-create head and tail
        ListNode head=null,tail=null;
        int carry=0;//to track carry value(prevNode.val>9)
        /*Its initially set to zero as for first node there wont exist any carry*/
        while(l1!=null&&l2!=null)
        {
            ListNode current = new ListNode();
            int sum=+carry+l1.val+l2.val;//IMPORTANT
            current.val=sum%10;//maintains value of node's value within 9
            carry=sum/10;//carry =>1 only if sum>9
            if(head==null)
            {
                head=tail=current;
            }
            else
            {
                tail.next=current;
                tail=current;
            }
            l1=l1.next;
            l2=l2.next;
        }
        /*After big loop well still be using carry condition cause its possible that after its completion,we get carry =1 and upcoming nodes are already 9 so it would cause an error to prevent this continue with carry logic*/
        while(l1!=null)
        {
            int k=carry+l1.val;
            l1.val=k%10;
            carry=k/10;
            tail.next=l1;//dont create new node[Recycle!!]
            tail=l1;
            l1=l1.next;
        }
         while(l2!=null)
        {
            int k=carry+l2.val;
            l2.val=k%10;
            carry=k/10;
            tail.next=l2;
            tail=l2;
            l2=l2.next;
        }
        /* now after compelete cycle its possible that our carry is stil one
        eg:9->9->9->NULL
           1->NULL
           so after compelete cycle our LL is 
           0->0->0->Null
           so we need to add a new node to make 
           0->0->0->1->Null
           */
        if(carry==1)
        {
            ListNode current = new ListNode();
            current.val=1;
            tail.next=current;
        }
        return head;
    }
}

 * Definition for singly-linked list.
 * struct ListNode {
 *     int val;
 *     ListNode *next;
 *     ListNode() : val(0), next(nullptr) {}
 *     ListNode(int x) : val(x), next(nullptr) {}
 *     ListNode(int x, ListNode *next) : val(x), next(next) {}
 * };
 */
class Solution {
public:
    ListNode* reverse(ListNode*head) {
        
       ListNode* curr = head;
       ListNode* prev = NULL;
       ListNode* forward= curr;
        
        while(curr != NULL) {
            forward = curr -> next;
            curr -> next = prev;
            prev = curr;
            curr = forward;
        }
        return prev;
    }
     void insertAtTail(ListNode* &head,ListNode* &tail, int val) {
        
       ListNode* temp= new ListNode(val);
        //empty list
        if(head == NULL) {
            head = temp;
            tail = temp;
            return;
        }
        else
        {
            tail -> next = temp;
            tail = temp;
        }
    }

       ListNode* add(ListNode* first,ListNode* second) {
        int carry = 0;
        
       ListNode*ansHead = NULL;
       ListNode*ansTail = NULL;
        
        while(first != NULL || second != NULL || carry != 0) {
            
            int val1 = 0;
            if(first != NULL)
                val1 = first -> val;
                
            int val2 = 0;
            if(second !=NULL)
                val2 = second -> val;
            
            
            int sum = carry + val1 + val2;
            
            int digit = sum%10;
            
            //create node and add in answer Linked List
            insertAtTail(ansHead, ansTail, digit);
            
            carry = sum/10;
            if(first != NULL)
                first = first -> next;
            
            if(second != NULL)
                second = second -> next;
        }
        return ansHead;
    }
    
    ListNode* addTwoNumbers(ListNode* l1, ListNode* l2) {
        l1 = reverse(l1);
        l2 = reverse(l2);
        
        //step2 - add 2 LL
       ListNode* ans = add(l1, l2);
        
        //step 3 
        
        
        return ans;
    }
};

9/29/23, 09:55 - Satwik Geu: public List<Integer> majorityElement(int[] nums) {
	List<Integer> result = new ArrayList<Integer>();
	if (nums.length == 0)
		return result;
	// In the begining, both Trump and Biden don't get a vote
	int firstMajor = Integer.MAX_VALUE, firstSum = 0, secondMajor = Integer.MIN_VALUE, secondSum = 0;
	
	for (int i = 0; i < nums.length; i++) {
		// case 1: I want to vote for Biden or Trump
		if (nums[i] == firstMajor)
			firstSum++;
		else if (nums[i] == secondMajor)
			secondSum++;
		// case 2: I want to run for the president
		else if (firstSum == 0) {
			firstMajor = nums[i];
			firstSum = 1;
		}
		else if (secondSum == 0) {
			secondMajor = nums[i];
			secondSum = 1;
		}
		// case 3: fuck sleepy Joe and crazy Trump, let James be the president
		else {
			firstSum--;
			secondSum--;
		}
	}
	// After election, we need to count the vote again.
	firstSum = 0;
	secondSum = 0;
	for (int i = 0; i < nums.length; i++) {
		if (nums[i] == firstMajor)
			firstSum++;    
		else if (nums[i] == secondMajor)
			secondSum++;
	}
	if (firstSum > nums.length / 3)
		result.add(firstMajor);
	if (secondSum > nums.length / 3)
		result.add(secondMajor);
	return result;
}

// Function to create a new Node
// with given data
struct Node* createnode(int data)
{
	struct Node* newnode =(struct Node*)malloc(sizeof(struct Node));
	newnode->data = data;
	newnode->next = NULL;
	return newnode;
}

// Function to insert a Node at the end of LL

void insert(struct Node** head, int val)
{
      struct  Node* new=createnode(val);
      if(*head==NULL)
      {
        *head=new;
        return;
      }
      struct Node* temp=*head;
      while(temp->next!=NULL)
      {
          temp=temp->next;
      }
      temp->next=new;

}

// Function to reverse the linked list and return
// its length
int reverse(struct Node** head_ref)
{
	struct Node* prev = NULL;
	struct Node* current = *head_ref;
	struct Node* next;
	int len = 0;
	while (current != NULL) {
		len++;
		next = current->next;
		current->next = prev;
		prev = current;
		current = next;
	}
	*head_ref = prev;
	return len;
}

// Function to make an empty linked list of
// given size
struct Node* make_empty_list(int size)
{
	struct Node* head = NULL;
	while (size--)
		insert(&head, 0);
	return head;
}

// Multiply contents of two linked lists => store
// in another list and return its head
struct Node* multiplyTwoLists(struct Node* first,struct Node* second)
{
	int m = reverse(&first), n = reverse(&second);
	struct Node* result = make_empty_list(m + n + 1);
	struct Node *second_ptr = second,
		*result_ptr1 = result, *result_ptr2, *first_ptr;

	// multiply each Node of second list with first
	while (second_ptr) {

		int carry = 0;
		// each time we start from the next of Node from which we started last time
		result_ptr2 = result_ptr1;
		first_ptr = first;
		while (first_ptr) {
			int mul = first_ptr->data * second_ptr->data+ carry;
			result_ptr2->data += mul % 10;
			carry = mul / 10 + result_ptr2->data / 10;
			result_ptr2->data = result_ptr2->data % 10;

			first_ptr = first_ptr->next;
			result_ptr2 = result_ptr2->next;
		}

		// if carry is remaining from last multiplication
		if (carry > 0) {
			result_ptr2->data += carry;
		}

		result_ptr1 = result_ptr1->next;
		second_ptr = second_ptr->next;
	}
	reverse(&result);
	reverse(&first);
	reverse(&second);

	// remove if there are zeros at starting
	while (result->data == 0) {
		struct Node* temp = result;
		result = result->next;
		free(temp);
	}

	// Return head of multiplication list
	return result;
}

        reverse(&l2);
       Node*res= NULL;
       Node*itr = NULL;
        
        while(l1!= NULL && l2!= NULL) {
            digit=l1->data+l2->data+carry;
            sum=digit%10;
            if(res==NULL)
            {
                res=createnode(sum);
                itr=res;
            }
            else
            {
                itr->next=createnode(sum);
                itr=itr->next;
            }
            carry=digit/10;
            l1=l1->next;
            l2=l2->next;
        }
        while(l1!=NULL)
        {
            sum=(l1->data+carry)%10;
            itr->next=createnode(sum);
            itr=itr->next;
            carry=(l1->data+carry)/10;
            l1=l1->next;
        }

        {
            sum=(l2->data+carry)%10;
            itr->next=createnode(sum);
            itr=itr->next;
            carry=(l2->data+carry)/10;
            l2=l2->next;
        }
        if(l1==NULL && l2==NULL)
        {
            if(carry!=0)
            {
                itr->next=createnode(carry);
                itr=itr->next;
            }
            itr->next=NULL;
        }
        reverse(&res);
        return res;
    }

// A utility function to print a linked list
void printList(struct Node* ptr)
{
	while (ptr != NULL) {
		printf("%d", ptr->data);
		if (ptr->next)
			printf("->");
		ptr = ptr->next;
	}
	printf("\n");
}

#include <stdlib.h>

typedef struct Node {
    int data;
    struct Node* next;
} Node;

Node* createNode(int data) {
    Node* newNode = (Node*)malloc(sizeof(Node));
    newNode->data = data;
    newNode->next = NULL;
    return newNode;
}

void insertEnd(Node** head, int data) {
    Node* newNode = createNode(data);
    if (*head == NULL) {
        *head = newNode;
        return;
    }
    Node* temp = *head;
    while (temp->next != NULL) {
        temp = temp->next;
    }
    temp->next = newNode;
}

void display(Node* head) {
    while (head != NULL) {
        printf("%d", head->data);
        head = head->next;
    }
}

Node* divideLists(Node* dividend, int divisor) {
    Node* result = NULL;
    Node* temp = NULL;
    int carry = 0;

    while (dividend != NULL) {
        int currentData = dividend->data + carry * 10;
        int quotient = currentData / divisor;
        carry = currentData % divisor;

        if (result == NULL && quotient == 0) {
            // Skip leading zeroes in the quotient
        } else {
            insertEnd(&result, quotient);
        }

        dividend = dividend->next;
    }

    return result;
}

int main() {
    Node* dividend = NULL;

    // Assuming dividend is 532
    insertEnd(&dividend, 1);
    insertEnd(&dividend, 0);
    insertEnd(&dividend, 0);
    
    

    int divisor = 10;

    printf("Dividend: ");
    display(dividend);
    printf("\nDivisor: %d\n", divisor);

    Node* result = divideLists(dividend, divisor);

    printf("Result: ");
    if (result != NULL) {
        display(result);
    } else {
        printf("0");
    }

    // Free memory
    while (dividend != NULL) {
        Node* temp = dividend;
        dividend = dividend->next;
        free(temp);
    }

    while (result != NULL) {
        Node* temp = result;
        result = result->next;
        free(temp);
    }

    return 0;
}

10/12/23, 22:57 - Gautam Aggarwal😌: #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

// Linked list Node
struct Node {
	int data;
	struct Node* next;
};

// Function to create a new Node
// with given data
struct Node* newNode(int data)
{
	struct Node* new_node =
		(struct Node*)malloc(sizeof(struct Node));
	new_node->data = data;
	new_node->next = NULL;
	return new_node;
}

// Function to insert a Node at the
// beginning of the Linked List
void insert(struct Node** head, int new_data)
{
      struct  Node* new=newNode(new_data);
      if(*head==NULL)
      {
        *head=new;
        return;
      }
      struct Node* temp=*head;
      while(temp->next!=NULL)
      {
          temp=temp->next;
      }
      temp->next=new;

}

// Function to reverse the linked list and return
// its length
int reverse(struct Node** head_ref)
{
	struct Node* prev = NULL;
	struct Node* current = *head_ref;
	struct Node* next;
	int len = 0;
	while (current != NULL) {
		len++;
		next = current->next;
		current->next = prev;
		prev = current;
		current = next;
	}
	*head_ref = prev;
	return len;
}

// Function to make an empty linked list of
// given size
struct Node* make_empty_list(int size)
{
	struct Node* head = NULL;
	while (size--)
		insert(&head, 0);
	return head;
}

// Multiply contents of two linked lists => store
// in another list and return its head
struct Node* multiplyTwoLists(struct Node* first,
						struct Node* second)
{
	// reverse the lists to multiply from end
	// m and n lengths of linked lists to make
	// and empty list
	int m = reverse(&first), n = reverse(&second);

	// make a list that will contain the result
	// of multiplication.
	// m+n+1 can be max size of the list
	struct Node* result = make_empty_list(m + n + 1);

	// pointers for traverse linked lists and also
	// to reverse them after
	struct Node *second_ptr = second,
		*result_ptr1 = result, *result_ptr2, *first_ptr;

	// multiply each Node of second list with first
	while (second_ptr) {

		int carry = 0;

		// each time we start from the next of Node
		// from which we started last time
		result_ptr2 = result_ptr1;

		first_ptr = first;

		while (first_ptr) {

			// multiply a first list's digit with a
			// current second list's digit
			int mul = first_ptr->data * second_ptr->data
					+ carry;

			// Assign the product to corresponding Node
			// of result
			result_ptr2->data += mul % 10;

			// now resultant Node itself can have more
			// than 1 digit
			carry = mul / 10 + result_ptr2->data / 10;
			result_ptr2->data = result_ptr2->data % 10;

			first_ptr = first_ptr->next;
			result_ptr2 = result_ptr2->next;
		}

		// if carry is remaining from last multiplication
		if (carry > 0) {
			result_ptr2->data += carry;
		}

		result_ptr1 = result_ptr1->next;
		second_ptr = second_ptr->next;
	}

	// reverse the result_list as it was populated
	// from last Node
	reverse(&result);
	reverse(&first);
	reverse(&second);

	// remove if there are zeros at starting
	while (result->data == 0) {
		struct Node* temp = result;
		result = result->next;
		free(temp);
	}

	// Return head of multiplication list
	return result;
}

// A utility function to print a linked list
void printList(struct Node* Node)
{
	while (Node != NULL) {
		printf("%d", Node->data);
		if (Node->next)
			printf("->");
		Node = Node->next;
	}
	printf("\n");
}

// Driver program to test above function
int main(void)
{
	struct Node* first = NULL;
	struct Node* second = NULL;

	// create first list 9->9->9->4->6->9
	insert(&first, 1);
	insert(&first, 2);
	insert(&first, 3);
	insert(&first, 4);
// 	push(&first, 0);
// 	push(&first, 0);
	printf("First List is: ");
	printList(first);

	// create second list 9->9->8->4->9
	insert(&second, 7);
	insert(&second, 8);
	insert(&second, 9);
// 	push(&second, 0);
// 	push(&second, 0);
	printf("Second List is: ");
	printList(second);

	// Multiply the two lists and see result
	struct Node* result = multiplyTwoLists(first, second);
	printf("Resultant list is: ");
	printList(result);

	return 0;
}

int compare(struct Node * n1,struct Node * n2 )
{
	int l1=getLength(n1);
	int l2=getLength(n2);
	if(l1>l2)
		return 1;
	else if(l2>l1)
	{
		return -1;
	}
	else{
		struct Node *itr1=n1,*itr2=n2;
		while(itr1!=NULL)
		{
			if(itr1->data>itr2->data)
			{
				return 1;
			}
			else if(itr1->data<itr2->data)
			{
				return -1;
			}
			itr1=itr1->next;
			itr2=itr2->next;
		}
		return 0;
	}
}

// Print function
void printList(struct Node* ptr)
{
	while (ptr != NULL) {
		printf("%d ", ptr->data);
		ptr = ptr->next;
	}
	printf("\n");
}
struct Node * continueD(struct Node *n1,struct Node *n2)
{
	
	int comp=compare(n1,n2);
	if(comp==0)
	{
		return createnode(1);
	}
	if(comp==-1)
	{
		return createnode(0);
	}
	Node* count=createnode(0);
	Node*  adder=createnode(1);	
	Node* result=NULL;	
	do
	{
		result=subtractLinkedList(n1,n2);
		count=Add(count,adder);
	}while(compare(result,n2)>=1);
	printList(count);
	return count;
}

10/18/23, 19:27 - Gautam Aggarwal😌: struct node* createnode(int data)
{
	struct node* new =(struct node*)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
	new->data = data;
	new->next = NULL;
	return new;
}

void insert(Node** head, int val) {
     Node* new = createnode(val);
    if (*head == NULL) {
        *head = new;
         return ;
    }
     Node* temp = *head;
    while (temp->next != NULL) {
        temp = temp->next;
    }
    temp->next = new;
}

// Function to reverse the linked list and return its length
int rev(struct node** head)
{
	 Node* prev = NULL;
	 Node* forward;
	 Node* curr = *head;
	int len=0;
	while (curr!=NULL) {
		len++;
		forward=curr->next;
		curr->next=prev;
		prev=curr;
		curr=forward;
	}
	*head=prev;
	return len;
}
// Function to make an empty linked list of given size to store the result 
Node* newlist(int size)
{
	 Node* head = NULL;
	while (size--)
	{
		insert(&head,0);
	}
	return head;
}

// MULTIPLY LOGIC
 Node* multiply( Node* first, Node* second ,int n,int m,int k)
{
	
	 Node* result = newlist(m + n + 1);
	 Node *ptr2 = second,*resptr1 = result, *resptr2, *ptr1;

	// multiply each Node of second list with first
	while (ptr2) {

		int carry = 0;
		// each time we start from the next of Node from which we started last time
		resptr2 = resptr1;
		ptr1 = first;
		while (ptr1) {
			int mul = ptr1->data * ptr2->data+ carry;
			resptr2->data += mul % 10;
			carry = mul / 10 + resptr2->data / 10;
			resptr2->data = resptr2->data % 10;

			ptr1 = ptr1->next;
			resptr2 = resptr2->next;
		}
		// if carry is remaining from last multiplication
		if (carry > 0) {
			resptr2->data += carry;
		}
		resptr1 = resptr1->next;
		ptr2 = ptr2->next;
	}
	 rev(&result);
	// reverse(&first);
	// reverse(&second);
	// remove if there are zeros at starting
	while (result->data == 0) {
		struct node* temp = result;
		result = result->next;
		free(temp);
	}
    rev(&result);
	return result;
}

struct BigInteger mul(struct BigInteger a,struct BigInteger b)
{
    struct node * first=a.head;
    struct node *second=b.head;
    int k=0;
    struct BigInteger result;
    result.head=multiply(first,second,a.length,b.length,k);
    return result;
}

#include <stdlib.h>

typedef struct node{
    int data;
    struct node* next;
}Node;

struct BigInteger {
    struct node *head;
    int length;
    int sign;
};
struct BigInteger sub(struct BigInteger , struct BigInteger ) ;
struct BigInteger add(struct BigInteger , struct BigInteger ) ;
struct BigInteger initialize(char *s) {
    struct BigInteger num;
    num.sign = 1;
    num.head = NULL;
    num.length = 0;

    int i = 0;
    if (s[i] == '-') {
        num.sign = -1;
        i++;
    }

    while (s[i] != '\0') {
        struct node* newNode = (struct node*)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
        newNode->data = s[i] - '0';  // Convert character to integer
        newNode->next = num.head;    // Set next pointer
        num.head = newNode;          // Update head pointer
        num.length++;
        i++;
    }

    return num;
}


void reverse(struct BigInteger* num) {
    struct node* forward = NULL;
    struct node* curr = num->head;
    struct node* prev = NULL;
    while (curr != NULL) {
        forward = curr->next;
        curr->next = prev;
        prev = curr;
        curr = forward;
    }
    num->head = prev;
}

int compareAbs(struct BigInteger a, struct BigInteger b) {
    // Compare the lengths of a and b first
    if (a.length < b.length) {
        return -1;
    } else if (a.length > b.length) {
        return 1;
    }

    struct node* A = a.head;
    struct node* B = b.head;

    while (A != NULL && B != NULL) {
        if (A->data < B->data) {
            return -1;
        } else if (A->data > B->data) {
            return 1;
        }

        A = A->next;
        B = B->next;
    }

    return 0; 
}

struct BigInteger* create()
{
    struct BigInteger*num=(struct BigInteger*)malloc(sizeof(struct BigInteger));
    if(num==NULL)
    {
        printf("memory allocation failed\n");
        exit(1);
    }
    num->head=NULL;
    num->sign='+';
    num->length=0;
    return num;
}

struct BigInteger add(struct BigInteger a, struct BigInteger b) {
    struct BigInteger result;
    result.head = NULL;
    result.length = 0;

    // // Handle the signs of a and b
    // if (a.sign == -1 && b.sign == 1) {
    //     a.sign = 1;
    //     result = sub(b, a);
    // } else if (a.sign == 1 && b.sign == -1) {
    //     b.sign = 1;
    //     result = sub(a, b);
    // } else {
    //     result.sign = a.sign;
        struct node* A = a.head;
        struct node* B = b.head;
        struct node* prev = NULL;
        int carry = 0;

        while (A != NULL || B != NULL || carry) {
            int sum;
            if (A != NULL && B != NULL) {
                 sum = carry + A->data + B->data;
                } 
                else if (A != NULL) {
                          sum = carry + A->data;
                    } 
                    else if (B != NULL) {
                      sum = carry + B->data;
                    }
                    else {
                          sum = carry;
                    }
            if (A) {
                A = A->next;
            }
            if (B) {
                B = B->next;
            }

            struct node* newNode = (struct node*)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
            newNode->data = sum % 10;
            newNode->next = NULL;

            if (prev == NULL) {
                result.head=newNode;
            } 
            else {
                prev->next=newNode;
            }
            prev=newNode;
            carry=sum / 10;
            result.length++;
        }
    return result;
}

// Function to insert  Node at the end of LL

struct node* createnode(int data)
{
	struct node* new =(struct node*)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
	new->data = data;
	new->next = NULL;
	return new;
}

void insert(Node** head, int val) {
     Node* new = createnode(val);
    if (*head == NULL) {
        *head = new;
         return ;
    }
     Node* temp = *head;
    while (temp->next != NULL) {
        temp = temp->next;
    }
    temp->next = new;
}

// Function to reverse the linked list and return its length
int rev(struct node** head)
{
	 Node* prev = NULL;
	 Node* forward;
	 Node* curr = *head;
	int len=0;
	while (curr!=NULL) {
		len++;
		forward=curr->next;
		curr->next=prev;
		prev=curr;
		curr=forward;
	}
	*head=prev;
	return len;
}
// Function to make an empty linked list of given size to store the result 
Node* newlist(int size)
{
	 Node* head = NULL;
	while (size--)
	{
		insert(&head,0);
	}
	return head;
}

// MULTIPLY LOGIC
 Node* multiply( Node* first, Node* second ,int n,int m,int k)
{
	
	 Node* result = newlist(m + n + 1);
	 Node *ptr2 = second,*resptr1 = result, *resptr2, *ptr1;

	// multiply each Node of second list with first
	while (ptr2) {

		int carry = 0;
		// each time we start from the next of Node from which we started last time
		resptr2 = resptr1;
		ptr1 = first;
		while (ptr1) {
			int mul = ptr1->data * ptr2->data+ carry;
			resptr2->data += mul % 10;
			carry = mul / 10 + resptr2->data / 10;
			resptr2->data = resptr2->data % 10;

			ptr1 = ptr1->next;
			resptr2 = resptr2->next;
		}
		// if carry is remaining from last multiplication
		if (carry > 0) {
			resptr2->data += carry;
		}
		resptr1 = resptr1->next;
		ptr2 = ptr2->next;
	}
	 rev(&result);
	// reverse(&first);
	// reverse(&second);
	// remove if there are zeros at starting
	while (result->data == 0) {
		struct node* temp = result;
		result = result->next;
		free(temp);
	}
    rev(&result);
	return result;
}

struct BigInteger mul(struct BigInteger a,struct BigInteger b)
{
    struct node * first=a.head;
    struct node *second=b.head;
    int k=0;
    struct BigInteger result;
    result.head=multiply(first,second,a.length,b.length,k);
    return result;
}

void display(struct BigInteger num) {
    // if (num.sign == -1) {
    //     printf("-");
    // }  
    reverse(&num);
    struct node *ptr = num.head;
    while (ptr!= NULL) 
    {
        printf("%d", ptr->data);
        ptr= ptr->next;
    }
    printf("\n");
}

11/22/23, 22:55 - Satwik Geu: #include<stdio.h>
#include<stdlib.h>
typedef struct node
{
    int key;
    int val;
    struct node * next;
}node;
//add
void add(node * a[],int len,int key,int val)
{
    node * curr=(node *)malloc(sizeof(node));
    curr->next=NULL;
    curr->key=key;
    curr->val=val;
    int ind=key%len;
    if(a[ind]==NULL)
    {
        a[ind]=curr;
    }
    else
    {
        node * itr=a[ind];
        while(itr!=NULL)
        {
            if(itr->key==key)
            {
                itr->val=val;
                return;
            }
            itr=itr->next;
        }
        curr->next=a[ind];
        a[ind]=curr;
    }
}
//delete
void delete(node * a[],int len,int key)
{
    int ind=key%len;
    node * itr=a[ind];
    node * prev=NULL;
    if(itr->key==key)
    {
        a[ind]=itr->next;
        return ;
    }
    while(itr!=NULL)
    {
        if(itr->key==key)
        {
            prev->next=itr->next;
            break;
        }
        prev=itr;
        itr=itr->next;
    }
}
//get
int get(node * a[],int len,int key)
{
    int ans=-1;
    int ind=key%len;
    node * itr=a[ind];
    while(itr!=NULL)
    {
        if(itr->key==key)
        {
            ans=itr->val;
            break;
        }
        itr=itr->next;
    }
    return ans;
}
int main()
{
    int len=10;
    node * a[10];
    int size=0;
    for(int i=0;i<len;i++)
    {
        a[i]=NULL;
    }
    add(a,10,15,102);
    add(a,10,15,103);
    add(a,10,5,104);
    printf("%d\n",get(a,len,5));
    printf("%d\n",get(a,len,15));
    delete(a,len,5);
    delete(a,len,15);
    delete(a,len,15);
    printf("%d",get(a,len,5));
    printf("%d",get(a,len,5));
    printf("%d",get(a,len,15));
}

11/23/23, 13:29 - Satwik Geu: #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

typedef struct node {
    int data;
    struct node* next;
} node;

void insert(node** head, int data) {
    node* curr = (node*)malloc(sizeof(node));
    curr->data = data;
    curr->next = NULL;
    if (*head == NULL) {
        *head = curr;
    } else {
        node* itr = *head;
        while (itr->next != NULL) {
            itr = itr->next;
        }
        itr->next = curr;
    }
}

void print(node* head) {
    if (head == NULL) {
        printf("List is empty.\n");
        return;
    }
    while (head != NULL) {
        printf("%d,", head->data);
        head = head->next;
    }
    printf("\n");
}

void part(node** head, int v) {
    node* h1 = NULL, *t1 = NULL;
    node* h2 = NULL, *t2 = NULL;
    node* itr = *head;

    while (itr != NULL) {
        if (itr->data < v) {
            if (h1 == NULL) {
                h1 = t1 = itr;
            } else {
                t1->next = itr;
                t1 = t1->next;
            }
        } else {
            if (h2 == NULL) {
                h2 = t2 = itr;
            } else {
                t2->next = itr;
                t2 = t2->next;
            }
        }
        itr = itr->next;
    }

    if (h1 == NULL) {
        *head = h2;
    } else {
        t1->next = h2;
        if (h2 != NULL) {
            t2->next = NULL;
        }
        *head = h1;
    }
}

int main() {
    node* head = NULL;
    int choice, data, value;

    do {
        printf("\nMenu:\n");
        printf("1. Insert\n");
        printf("2. Partition\n");
        printf("3. Display\n");
        printf("4. Exit\n");
        printf("Enter your choice: ");
        scanf("%d", &choice);

        switch (choice) {
            case 1:
                printf("Enter data to insert: ");
                scanf("%d", &data);
                insert(&head, data);
                break;
            case 2:
                printf("Enter value for partition: ");
                scanf("%d", &value);
                part(&head, value);
                break;
            case 3:
                printf("List: ");
                print(head);
                break;
            case 4:
                printf("Exiting program.\n");
                break;
            default:
                printf("Invalid choice. Please enter a valid option.\n");
        }
    } while (choice != 4);

    return 0;
}

11/23/23, 23:43 - Satwik Geu: #include<stdio.h>
#include<stdlib.h>
typedef struct node
{
    int key;
    int val;
    struct node * next;
}node;
//add
void add(node * a[],int len,int key,int val)
{
    node * curr=(node *)malloc(sizeof(node));
    curr->next=NULL;
    curr->key=key;
    curr->val=val;
    int ind=key%len;
    if(a[ind]==NULL)
    {
        a[ind]=curr;
    }
    else
    {
        node * itr=a[ind];
        while(itr!=NULL)
        {
            if(itr->key==key)
            {
                itr->val=val;
                return;
            }
            itr=itr->next;
        }
        curr->next=a[ind];
        a[ind]=curr;
    }
}
//delete
void delete(node * a[],int len,int key)
{
    int ind=key%len;
    node * itr=a[ind];
    node * prev=NULL;
    if(itr->key==key)
    {
        a[ind]=itr->next;
        return ;
    }
    while(itr!=NULL)
    {
        if(itr->key==key)
        {
            prev->next=itr->next;
            break;
        }
        prev=itr;
        itr=itr->next;
    }
}
//get
int get(node * a[],int len,int key)
{
    int ans=-1;
    int ind=key%len;
    node * itr=a[ind];
    while(itr!=NULL)
    {
        if(itr->key==key)
        {
            ans=itr->val;
            break;
        }
        itr=itr->next;
    }
    return ans;
}
int main()
{
    int len=10;
    node * a[10];
    int size=0;
    for(int i=0;i<len;i++)
    {
        a[i]=NULL;
    }
    add(a,10,15,102);
    add(a,10,15,103);
    add(a,10,5,104);
    printf("%d\n",get(a,len,5));
    printf("%d\n",get(a,len,15));
    delete(a,len,5);
    delete(a,len,15);
    delete(a,len,15);
    printf("%d",get(a,len,5));
    printf("%d",get(a,len,5));
    printf("%d",get(a,len,15));
}

11/28/23, 20:48 - Satwik Geu: Q10. Using circular linked list allocate time slots of 10ms for given processes in time sharing Environment and then print which process will be completed in how much time.

*/
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
struct Process
{
    int process_id;
    int remaining_time;
    struct Process *next;
};
struct Process *create_Process(int p_id, int r_time)
{
    struct Process *new_process = (struct Process *)malloc(sizeof(struct Process));
    new_process->process_id = p_id;
    new_process->remaining_time = r_time;
    new_process->next = NULL;

    return new_process;
}
void add_process(struct Process **p, int p_id, int r_time)
{
    struct Process *new_process = create_Process(p_id, r_time);
    if (*p == NULL)
    {
        *p = new_process;
        (*p)->next = *p;
    }
    else
    {
        struct Process *temp = *p;
        while (temp->next != *p)
        {
            temp = temp->next;
        }
        temp->next = new_process;
        new_process->next = *p;
    }
    return;
} // inserting the process at the end
void schedule_time_slots(struct Process *p)
{
    if (p == NULL)
    {
        printf("\nNo processes available.");
        return;
    }
    struct Process *current = p;
    printf("\n\nProcessId\t\tTime Completed\t\tTime Remaining\n");
    while (current->next != p || current->next->remaining_time > 0)
    {
        if (current->remaining_time > 0)
        {
            printf("%d\t\t\t", current->process_id);
            if (current->remaining_time >= 10)
            {
                printf("%d\t\t\t", 10);
                current->remaining_time -= 10;
                printf("%d\n", current->remaining_time);
            }
            else
            {
                printf("%d\t\t\t", current->remaining_time);
                current->remaining_time = 0;
                printf("%d\n", current->remaining_time);
            }
        }
        current = current->next;
    }
}
void displayMenu()
{
    printf("\n****INPUT***\n");
    printf("\nMenu:\n");
    printf("1. Add a Process\n");
    printf("2. Schedule Time Slots\n");
    printf("3. Exit\n");
}
int main()
{
    struct Process *p = NULL;
    int pro_id, rem_time;
    int choice;
    do
    {
        displayMenu();
        printf("Enter Your Choice :: ");
        scanf("%d", &choice);

        switch (choice)
        {
        case 1:
            printf("\nEnter Process Id :: ");
            scanf("%d", &pro_id);
            add_process(&p, pro_id, 10);
            printf("****OUTPUT****\n");
            printf("\nProcess Added Successfully.");
            break;
        case 2:
            printf("****OUTPUT****\n");
            printf("\nScheduling Time Slots");
            schedule_time_slots(p);
            break;
        case 3:
            printf("****OUTPUT****\n");
            printf("\nExited");
            break;
        default:
            printf("****OUTPUT****\n");
            printf("\nInvalid Choice! Try Again");
            break;
        }
    } while (choice != 3);
    return 0;
}

11/30/23, 21:22 - Gautam Aggarwal😌: /*
    Q11. Write a C program to store the details of a weighted graph (Use array of pointers concept).
*/

#include<stdio.h>
#include<stdlib.h>

typedef struct Pair{
    int node;
    int weight;
    struct Pair *next;
}Pair;

void insertNode(Pair *graph[], int source, int node, int weight)
{
    Pair *newNode = (Pair *)malloc(sizeof(Pair));
    newNode -> node = node;
    newNode -> weight = weight;
    newNode -> next = NULL;
    Pair *sourceNode = graph[source];
    if(!sourceNode)
        graph[source] = newNode;
    else
    {
        while(sourceNode -> next)
            sourceNode = sourceNode -> next;
        sourceNode -> next = newNode;
    }
}

void display(Pair *graph[], int n)
{
    for(int i = 0; i<n; i++)
    {
        Pair *node = graph[i];
        while(node)
        {
            printf("%d -> (Node = %d, Weight = %d)\n", i, node -> node, node -> weight);
            node = node -> next;
        }
    }
}

int main()
{
    int ch, source, weight, dest;
    Pair *graph[100] = {NULL};
    do
    {
        printf("Enter your choice(1 = insert, 2 = display): ");
        scanf("%d", &ch);

        switch (ch)
        {
            case 1:
                printf("Enter the source: ");
                scanf("%d", &source);
                printf("Enter the weight: ");
                scanf("%d", &weight);
                printf("Enter the destination: ");
                scanf("%d", &dest);
                insertNode(graph, source, dest, weight);
                printf("%d -> (%d, %d) inserted\n", source, dest, weight);
                break;
            case 2:
                display(graph, 100);
                break;
            default:
                break;
        }
    } while (ch);
    

    return 0;
}

12/7/23, 14:21 - Gautam Aggarwal😌: /*
Q8.Create a Base class that consists of private, protected and public data members and member functions.
Try using different access modifiers for inheriting Base class to the Derived class and create a table that summarizes the above three modes (when derived in public, protected and private modes) and shows the access specifier of the members of base class in the Derived class.*/
#include <iostream>
using namespace std;

#include <iostream>
using namespace std;

// Base class definition
class Base {
private:
    int privateData;  // Private member variable
protected:
    int protectedData;  // Protected member variable
public:
    int publicData;  // Public member variable

    // Default constructor
    Base() {
        privateData = 0;
        protectedData = 0;
        publicData = 0;
    }

    // Function to set data in the base class
    void getdata(int priv, int pro, int pub) {
        privateData = priv;
        protectedData = pro;
        publicData = pub;
    }

    // Function to display data of the base class
    void display() {
        cout << "Base Class - private: " << privateData;
        cout << ", protected: " << protectedData;
        cout << ", public: " << publicData << endl;
    }
};

// DerivedPublic class inherits publicly from Base
class DerivedPublic : public Base {
public:
    // Function to access base class members in DerivedPublic
    void accessBaseMembers() {
        cout << "DerivedPublic Class - Accessing Base Class members: ";
        // All members are accessible in the derived class
        //cout << "private: " << privateData;  // Not Accessible
        cout << ", protected: " << protectedData;
        cout << ", public: " << publicData << endl;
    }
};

// DerivedProtected class inherits protectedly from Base
class DerivedProtected : protected Base {
public:
    // Function to access base class members in DerivedProtected
    void accessBaseMembers() {
        cout << "DerivedProtected Class - Accessing Base Class members: ";
        // All members are accessible in the derived class
        //cout << "private: " << privateData;  // Not Accessible
        cout << ", protected: " << protectedData;
        cout << ", public: " << publicData << endl;
    }
};

// DerivedPrivate class inherits privately from Base
class DerivedPrivate : private Base {
public:
    // Function to access base class members in DerivedPrivate
    void accessBaseMembers() {
        cout << "DerivedPrivate Class - Accessing Base Class members: ";
        // All members are accessible in the derived class
        //cout << "private: " << privateData;  // Not Accessible
        cout << ", protected: " << protectedData;
        cout << ", public: " << publicData << endl;
    }
};

// Main function
int main() {
    int privateInput, protectedInput, publicInput;

    // Creating an object of Base class
    Base baseObj;
    cout << "\t\t**********INPUT**********\n";
    // Input data for the Base class
    cout << "Enter private data for the Base class: ";
    cin >> privateInput;
    cout << "Enter protected data for the Base class: ";
    cin >> protectedInput;
    cout << "Enter public data for the Base class: ";
    cin >> publicInput;

    baseObj.getdata(privateInput, protectedInput, publicInput);  // Setting data in the base object
    cout << "\t\t**********OUTPUT**********\n";
    baseObj.display();  // Displaying data of the base object

    // Public Inheritance
    DerivedPublic derivedPublic;
    derivedPublic.accessBaseMembers();  // Accessing base members in DerivedPublic

    // Protected Inheritance
    DerivedProtected derivedProtected;
    derivedProtected.accessBaseMembers(); // Error - Not accessible outside the class

    // Private Inheritance
    DerivedPrivate derivedPrivate;
    derivedPrivate.accessBaseMembers(); // Error - Not accessible outside the class

    return 0;
}

12/7/23, 20:19 - Satwik Geu: /*Write a C++ file handling program to count and display the number of palindrome present in a text file "myfile.txt".*/
#include<iostream>
#include<fstream>
#include<algorithm>						//for using reverse function
#include<string>
using namespace std;
bool isPalin(string word)					//function to check palindrome
{
    string temp=word;
    std::reverse(word.begin(), word.end());
    return temp==word;					//comparing word and reversed
}
int main()
{
     //opening stored file
    ifstream in("C:/Users/dhruv/OneDrive/Documents/Assignments/myFile.txt");
    string content="",word="";
    int c=0;							//keeping count of palindromes
    while(in.eof()!=1)						//iterating through the file
    {
        in>>word;
        content+=" ";
        content+=word;
        if(isPalin(word)==1)					//if word is palindrome
        {
            cout<<"Palindrome word found!: "<<word<<endl;
            c++;							    //increment palindrome counter
        }
    }
    if(c==0)
    {
        cout<<"No Palindromes Found\n";				    //0 palindromes found
    }
    else
    {
        cout<<"In the File There Were "<<c<<" Palindromes\n";	//one or more found
    }
    cout<<"--------------------------------------------------------------------------\n";
}

12/9/23, 18:59 - Satwik Geu: #include<stdio.h>
#include<stdlib.h>
typedef struct node
{
    int data;
    struct node * next;
} node;
void insertNode(node * a[],int src,int dest)
{
    node * curr1=(node*)malloc(sizeof(node));
    // node * curr2=(node*)malloc(sizeof(node));
    curr1->data=dest;
    curr1->next=a[src];
    // curr2->data=src;
    // curr2->next=a[dest];
    a[src]=curr1;
    // a[dest]=curr2;
}
void displayGraph(node * a[],int n)
{
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    {
        printf("%d:->",i);
        node * itr=a[i];
        while(itr!=NULL)
        {
            printf(" %d ,",itr->data);
            itr=itr->next;
        }
        printf("\n");
    }
}
void dfs(node * a[],int v[],int curr)
{
    v[curr]=1;
    printf("%d ",curr);
    node * itr=a[curr];
    while(itr!=NULL)
    {
        if(v[itr->data]!=1)
        {
            dfs(a,v,itr->data);
        }
        itr=itr->next;
    }
}
void bfs(node * a[],int v[],int curr)
{
    int q[100]={0};
    q[0]=curr;
    int f=0,r=1;
    while(f<r)
    {
        int t=q[f++];
        printf(" %d ",t);
        v[t]=1;
        node * itr=a[t];
        while(itr)
        {
            if(v[itr->data]==0)
            {
                q[r++]=itr->data;
                v[itr->data]=1;
            }
            itr=itr->next;
        }
    }
}
int main()
{
    node * a[15];
    int n=15;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    {
        a[i]=NULL;
    }
    printf("Graph representation:\n");
    insertNode(a,0,1);
    insertNode(a,0,2);
    insertNode(a,0,3);
    insertNode(a,1,2);
    insertNode(a,2,4);
    insertNode(a,3,3);
    insertNode(a,3,2);
    insertNode(a,1,10);
    insertNode(a,10,11);
    insertNode(a,11,14);
    //insertNode(a,2,3);
    displayGraph(a,n);
    printf("DFS:\n");
    int v[15]={0};
    bfs(a,v,0);
}

12/12/23, 23:22 - Satwik Geu: #include<iostream>
#include<string>
using namespace std;
class student
{
    protected:
        string name;
        int roll;
    public:
        student(){}
        student(string n,int r)
        {
            name=n;
            roll=r;
        }
};
class marks:virtual protected student
{
    protected:
        int m[5];
    public:
        marks(){}
        marks(string n,int r,int m1,int m2,int m3,int m4,int m5):student(n,r)
        {
            m[0]=m1;
            m[1]=m2;
            m[2]=m3;
            m[3]=m4;
            m[4]=m5;
        }
};
 class extra:virtual protected student
 {
     protected:
         int m1,m2;
    public:
         extra(){}
         extra(string n,int r,int m1,int m2):student(n,r)
         {
            this->m1=m1;
            this->m2=m2;
         }
 };
class display : protected extra, protected marks
{
    public:
    display() {}
    display(string n, int r, int m1, int m2, int m3, int m4, int m5, int m6, int m7)
        : /*this part->*/student(n, r)/*<----*/, marks(n, r, m1, m2, m3, m4, m5), extra(n, r, m6, m7)
    {
    }

    void show()
    {
        cout << "Name: " << name << endl;
        cout << "Roll: " << roll << endl;
        cout << "Marks of core subjects:" << endl;
        for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++)
        {
            cout << m[i] << endl;
        }
        cout << "Extra: " << m1 << endl;
    }
};

 int main()
 {
      display d("satwik",10,1,2,3,4,5,6,7);
      d.show();
 }

3/13/24, 19:27 - Satwik Geu: int s = 1;
        int e = n;
        while(s <= e)
        {
            int mid = (s +e)/2;
            int lSum = (mid * (mid + 1)) / 2;
            int rSum = (n * (n + 1))/2 - lSum + mid;
            if(lSum == rSum)
            {
                return mid;
            }
            if(lSum > rSum)
            {
                e = mid - 1;
            }
            else
            {
                s = mid + 1;
            }
        }
        return -1;

4/25/24, 19:47 - Satwik Geu: Ninja is planing this ‘N’ days-long training schedule. Each day, he can perform any one of these three activities. (Running, Fighting Practice or Learning New Moves). Each activity has some merit points on each day. As Ninja has to improve all his skills, he can’t do the same activity in two consecutive days. Can you help Ninja find out the maximum merit points Ninja can earn?

You are given a 2D array of size N*3 ‘POINTS’ with the points corresponding to each day and activity. Your task is to calculate the maximum number of merit points that Ninja can earn.

For Example
If the given ‘POINTS’ array is [[1,2,5], [3 ,1 ,1] ,[3,3,3] ],the answer will be 11 as 5 + 3 + 3.
4/25/24, 19:47 - Satwik Geu: https://www.naukri.com/code360/problems/ninja%E2%80%99s-training_3621003?utm_source=striver&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=a_zcoursetuf&leftPanelTabValue=PROBLEM
4/25/24, 19:47 - Satwik Geu: import java.util.Arrays;

public class Solution {
    public static int ninjaTraining(int n, int points[][]) {
    int dp[][] = new int[n + 1][4];
    for(int itr[] : dp)
        Arrays.fill(itr, -1);   
    return helper(n , points , dp , 3);
    }
    public static int helper(int n , int mat[][] , int dp[][] , int last)
    {
        if(n == 0)
            return 0;
        if(dp[n][last] != -1)
            return dp[n][last];
        int maxAns = -1;
        for(int i = 0 ; i < 3; i++)
        {
            if(i != last)
            {
                maxAns = Math.max(maxAns, mat[n - 1][i] + helper(n - 1 , mat , dp , i));
            }
        }
        return dp[n][last] = maxAns; 
    }
}

5/4/24, 09:24 - Satwik Geu: class Main {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int[][] graph = {
            {0, 2, 99999, 9, 99999},
            {99999, 0, 8, 7, 6},
            {99999, 99999, 0, 99999, 2},
            {99999, 99999, -9, 0, 99999},
            {99999, 99999, 99999, 3, 0}
        };

        shortest_distance(graph);
    }

     public static void shortest_distance(int[][] matrix) {
        int n = matrix.length;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
                if (matrix[i][j] == -1) {
                    matrix[i][j] = (int)(1e9);
                }
                if (i == j) matrix[i][j] = 0;
            }
        }

        for (int k = 0; k < n; k++) {
            for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
                for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
                    matrix[i][j] = Math.min(matrix[i][j],
                                            matrix[i][k] + matrix[k][j]);
                }
            }
        }

        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
                if (matrix[i][j] == (int)(1e9)) {
                    matrix[i][j] = -1;
                }
            }
        }
        printMatrix(matrix);
    }

    public static void printMatrix(int[][] matrix) {
        int V = matrix.length;
        for (int i = 0; i < V; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < V; j++) {
                if (matrix[i][j] == 99999) {
                    System.out.print("∞ ");
                } else {
                    System.out.print(matrix[i][j] + " ");
                }
            }
            System.out.println();
        }
        System.out.println();
    }
}

6/6/24, 20:12 - Satwik Geu: class Solution {
    public boolean isNStraightHand(int[] hand, int k) 
    {
        if(hand.length % k != 0)
            return false;  
        HashMap<Integer,Integer> h = new HashMap<>();
        for(int i : hand)
            h.put(i , h.getOrDefault(i , 0) + 1);
        Arrays.sort(hand);
        for(int i : hand)
        {
            if(!h.containsKey(i))
                continue;
            for(int j = 0; j < k; j++)
            {
                if(!h.containsKey(i + j))
                    return false;
                if(h.get(i + j) == 1)
                    h.remove(i + j);
                else
                    h.put(i + j , h.get(i + j) - 1);
            }
        }
        return true; 
    }
}

8/23/24, 14:10 - Gautam Aggarwal😌: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

struct Process {
    int id;
    int at;  
    int bt;  
    int st;  
    int ct;  
    int tat; 
    int wt;  
    int rt;  
};

int main() {
    int n;
    cout << "Enter the number of processes: ";
    cin >> n;

    vector<Process> processes(n);
    cout << "Enter the Arrival Time and Burst Time for each process:\n";
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        processes[i].id = i + 1;
        cout << "Process " << processes[i].id << ": ";
        cin >> processes[i].at >> processes[i].bt;
    }

    priority_queue<pair<int, int>, vector<pair<int, int>>, greater<pair<int, int>>> pq;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        pq.push({processes[i].at, i});
    }

    int timer = 0;
    while (!pq.empty()) {
        int index = pq.top().second;
        pq.pop();

        while (timer < processes[index].at)
            timer++;
        
        processes[index].st = timer;
        processes[index].rt = processes[index].st - processes[index].at;
        processes[index].ct = timer + processes[index].bt;
        processes[index].tat = processes[index].ct - processes[index].at;
        processes[index].wt = processes[index].tat - processes[index].bt;
        timer += processes[index].bt;
    }

    cout << "\nProcess\tAT\tBT\tST\tCT\tTAT\tWT\tRT\n";
    for (const auto &p : processes) {
        cout << "P" << p.id << "\t" << p.at << "\t" << p.bt << "\t" 
             << p.st << "\t" << p.ct << "\t" << p.tat << "\t" 
             << p.wt << "\t" << p.rt << endl;
    }
}

8/23/24, 14:10 - Gautam Aggarwal😌: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

struct Process {
    int id;
    int at;  // Arrival Time
    int bt;  // Burst Time
    int st;  // Start Time
    int ct;  // Completion Time
    int tat; // Turnaround Time
    int wt;  // Waiting Time
    int rt;  // Response Time
};

bool compareByArrivalTime(const Process &a, const Process &b) {
    return a.at < b.at;
}

int main() {
    int n;
    cout << "Enter the number of processes: ";
    cin >> n;

    vector<Process> processes(n);
    cout << "Enter the Arrival Time and Burst Time for each process:\n";
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        processes[i].id = i + 1;
        cout << "Process " << processes[i].id << ": ";
        cin >> processes[i].at >> processes[i].bt;
    }

    // Sort processes by arrival time
    // sort(processes.begin(), processes.end(), compareByArrivalTime);

    vector<bool> completed(n, false);
    int timer = 0;
    int completedProcesses = 0;

    while (completedProcesses < n) {
        int shortestJobIndex = -1;
        int minBurstTime = INT_MAX;

        // Find the process with the shortest burst time among those that have arrived
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            if (processes[i].at <= timer && !completed[i]) {
                // Select the process with the longest remaining burst time,
                // and in case of a tie, select the one with the earlier arrival time
                if (processes[i].bt < minBurstTime || 
                    (processes[i].bt == minBurstTime && processes[i].at < processes[shortestJobIndex].at)) {
                     shortestJobIndex = i;
                    minBurstTime = processes[i].bt;
                }
        }
        }

        if (shortestJobIndex == -1) {
            // If no process has arrived yet, move the timer forward
            timer++;
        } else {
            // Process the selected process
            int index = shortestJobIndex;
            processes[index].st = timer;
            processes[index].rt = processes[index].st - processes[index].at;
            processes[index].ct = timer + processes[index].bt;
            processes[index].tat = processes[index].ct - processes[index].at;
            processes[index].wt = processes[index].tat - processes[index].bt;
            timer += processes[index].bt;
            completed[index] = true;
            completedProcesses++;
        }
    }

    cout << "\nProcess\tAT\tBT\tST\tCT\tTAT\tWT\tRT\n";
    for (const auto &p : processes) {
        cout << "P" << p.id << "\t" << p.at << "\t" << p.bt << "\t" 
             << p.st << "\t" << p.ct << "\t" << p.tat << "\t" 
             << p.wt << "\t" << p.rt << endl;
    }
}

8/23/24, 14:10 - Gautam Aggarwal😌: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

struct Process {
    int id;
    int at;  // Arrival Time
    int bt;  // Burst Time
    int st;  // Start Time
    int ct;  // Completion Time
    int tat; // Turnaround Time
    int wt;  // Waiting Time
    int rt;  // Response Time
};

bool compareByArrivalTime(const Process &a, const Process &b) {
    return a.at < b.at;
}

int main() {
    int n;
    cout << "Enter the number of processes: ";
    cin >> n;

    vector<Process> processes(n);
    cout << "Enter the Arrival Time and Burst Time for each process:\n";
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        processes[i].id = i + 1;
        cout << "Process " << processes[i].id << ": ";
        cin >> processes[i].at >> processes[i].bt;
    }

    // Sort processes by arrival time
    // sort(processes.begin(), processes.end(), compareByArrivalTime);

    vector<bool> completed(n, false);
    int timer = 0;
    int completedProcesses = 0;

    while (completedProcesses < n) {
        int longestJobIndex = -1;
        int maxBurstTime = INT_MIN;

        // Find the process with the shortest burst time among those that have arrived
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
           if (processes[i].at <= timer && !completed[i]) {
                // Select the process with the longest remaining burst time,
                // and in case of a tie, select the one with the earlier arrival time
                if (processes[i].bt > maxBurstTime || 
                    (processes[i].bt == maxBurstTime && processes[i].at < processes[longestJobIndex].at)) {

                    maxBurstTime = processes[i].bt;
                    longestJobIndex = i;
                }
        }
        }

        if (longestJobIndex == -1) {
            // If no process has arrived yet, move the timer forward
            timer++;
        } else {
            // Process the selected process
            int index = longestJobIndex;
            processes[index].st = timer;
            processes[index].rt = processes[index].st - processes[index].at;
            processes[index].ct = timer + processes[index].bt;
            processes[index].tat = processes[index].ct - processes[index].at;
            processes[index].wt = processes[index].tat - processes[index].bt;
            timer += processes[index].bt;
            completed[index] = true;
            completedProcesses++;
        }
    }

    cout << "\nProcess\tAT\tBT\tST\tCT\tTAT\tWT\tRT\n";
    for (const auto &p : processes) {
        cout << "P" << p.id << "\t" << p.at << "\t" << p.bt << "\t" 
             << p.st << "\t" << p.ct << "\t" << p.tat << "\t" 
             << p.wt << "\t" << p.rt << endl;
    }
}

8/23/24, 14:11 - Gautam Aggarwal😌: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

struct Process {
    int id;
    int at;  // Arrival Time
    int bt;  // Burst Time
    int st;  // Start Time
    int ct;  // Completion Time
    int tat; // Turnaround Time
    int wt;  // Waiting Time
    int rt;  // Response Time
    int remaining_bt; // Remaining Burst Time
};

bool compareByArrivalTime(const Process &a, const Process &b) {
    return a.at < b.at;
}

int main() {
    int n;
    cout << "Enter the number of processes: ";
    cin >> n;

    vector<Process> processes(n);
    cout << "Enter the Arrival Time and Burst Time for each process:\n";
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        processes[i].id = i + 1;
        cout << "Process " << processes[i].id << ": ";
        cin >> processes[i].at >> processes[i].bt;
        processes[i].remaining_bt = processes[i].bt;
    }

    vector<bool> completed(n, false);
    int timer = 0, completedProcesses = 0, currentProcess = -1, minBurstTime = INT_MAX;

    while (completedProcesses < n) {
        // Find the process with the shortest remaining burst time that has arrived
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            if (processes[i].at <= timer && !completed[i]) {
                // Select the process with the longest remaining burst time,
                // and in case of a tie, select the one with the earlier arrival time
                if (processes[i].remaining_bt < minBurstTime || 
                    (processes[i].remaining_bt == minBurstTime && processes[i].at < processes[currentProcess].at)) {
                    minBurstTime = processes[i].remaining_bt;
                    currentProcess = i;
                }
        }
        }

        if (currentProcess == -1) {
            // If no process is available, move the timer forward
            timer++;
        } else {
            // Process the current process for one unit of time
            if (processes[currentProcess].remaining_bt == processes[currentProcess].bt) {
                processes[currentProcess].st = timer;
                processes[currentProcess].rt = processes[currentProcess].st - processes[currentProcess].at;
            }

            processes[currentProcess].remaining_bt--;
            timer++;
            minBurstTime = processes[currentProcess].remaining_bt;

            if (processes[currentProcess].remaining_bt == 0) {
                processes[currentProcess].ct = timer;
                processes[currentProcess].tat = processes[currentProcess].ct - processes[currentProcess].at;
                processes[currentProcess].wt = processes[currentProcess].tat - processes[currentProcess].bt;
                completed[currentProcess] = true;
                completedProcesses++;
                minBurstTime = INT_MAX;  // Reset for the next process
                currentProcess = -1;
            }
        }
    }

    cout << "\nProcess\tAT\tBT\tST\tCT\tTAT\tWT\tRT\n";
    for (const auto &p : processes) {
        cout << "P" << p.id << "\t" << p.at << "\t" << p.bt << "\t" 
             << p.st << "\t" << p.ct << "\t" << p.tat << "\t" 
             << p.wt << "\t" << p.rt << endl;
    }
}

LRTF
8/23/24, 14:12 - Gautam Aggarwal😌: //hrr
#include <iostream>
#include <vector>
using namespace std;

struct Process {
    int id;
    int at;  // Arrival Time
    int bt;  // Burst Time
    int st;  // Start Time
    int ct;  // Completion Time
    int tat; // Turnaround Time
    int wt;  // Waiting Time
    int rt;  // Response Time
    bool completed;
};

float calculate_response_ratio(const Process& p, int current_time) {
    float waiting_time = current_time - p.at;
    return (waiting_time + p.bt) / (float)p.bt;
}

int main() {
    int n, current_time = 0, completed = 0;
    float total_waiting_time = 0, total_turnaround_time = 0;
    float total_response_time = 0, total_idle_time = 0;
    float avg_waiting_time, avg_turnaround_time, avg_response_time, cpu_utilization, throughput;

    cout << "Enter the number of processes: ";
    cin >> n;

    vector<Process> processes(n);

    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        processes[i].id = i + 1;
        cout << "Enter arrival time and burst time for process " << processes[i].id << ": ";
        cin >> processes[i].at >> processes[i].bt;
        processes[i].completed = false;
    }

    while (completed != n) {
        int highest_rr_index = -1;
        float highest_rr = -1.0;

        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            if (processes[i].at <= current_time && !processes[i].completed) {
                float rr = calculate_response_ratio(processes[i], current_time);
                if (rr > highest_rr) {
                    highest_rr = rr;
                    highest_rr_index = i;
                }
            }
        }

        if (highest_rr_index == -1) {
            current_time++;
            total_idle_time++;
            continue;
        }

        int idx = highest_rr_index;
        processes[idx].st = current_time;
        processes[idx].ct = processes[idx].st + processes[idx].bt;
        processes[idx].tat = processes[idx].ct - processes[idx].at;
        processes[idx].wt = processes[idx].tat - processes[idx].bt;
        processes[idx].rt = processes[idx].st - processes[idx].at;

        total_waiting_time += processes[idx].wt;
        total_turnaround_time += processes[idx].tat;
        total_response_time += processes[idx].rt;

        current_time = processes[idx].ct;
        processes[idx].completed = true;
        completed++;
    }

    avg_waiting_time = total_waiting_time / n;
    avg_turnaround_time = total_turnaround_time / n;
    avg_response_time = total_response_time / n;
    cpu_utilization = ((current_time - total_idle_time) / (float)current_time) * 100;
    throughput = (float)n / current_time;

    cout << "\nProcess\tAT\tBT\tST\tCT\tTAT\tWT\tRT\n";
    for (const auto& p : processes) {
        cout << "P" << p.id << "\t" << p.at << "\t" << p.bt << "\t" 
             << p.st << "\t" << p.ct << "\t" << p.tat << "\t" 
             << p.wt << "\t" << p.rt << endl;
    }

    cout << "\nAverage Waiting Time: " << avg_waiting_time;
    cout << "\nAverage Turnaround Time: " << avg_turnaround_time;
    cout << "\nAverage Response Time: " << avg_response_time;
    cout << "\nCPU Utilization: " << cpu_utilization << "%";
    cout << "\nThroughput: " << throughput << " processes/unit time\n";

    return 0;
}

9/21/24, 21:37 - Satwik Geu: #include <iostream>
#include <unordered_set>

using namespace std;

unordered_set<int> solve(int a) {
    unordered_set<int> candidates;
    for (int i = 1; i * i <= a; i++) {
        if (a % i == 0) {
            if (i % 2 == 0) // segment len should be even
                candidates.insert(i);
            if ((a / i) % 2 == 0)
                candidates.insert(a / i);
        }
    }
    unordered_set<int> answer;
    for (int i : candidates) {
        answer.insert(1 + i / 2);
    }
    return answer;
}

int main() {
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    for (int _ = 1; _ <= t; _++) {
        int n, pos;
        cin >> n >> pos;
        unordered_set<int> candidates = solve(n - pos);  // bug2
        for (int i : solve(n + pos - 2)) { // bug1
            candidates.insert(i);
        }
        int answer = 0;
        for (int i : candidates) {
            if (i >= pos) {
                answer++;
            }
        }
        cout << answer << endl;
    }
}

9/22/24, 19:29 - Satwik Geu: #include <iostream>
#include <queue>
#include <string>
#include <vector>
using namespace std;

string minimalString(string s) {
    string pre = "";    // Empty string pre
    string post = "";   // Empty string post
    
    // Min-heap to keep track of remaining characters in the string
    priority_queue<char, vector<char>, greater<char>> minHeap;

    // Push all characters into the heap initially
    for (char c : s) {
        minHeap.push(c);
    }

    // Iterate through the string
    for (char c : s) {
        pre += c;      // Append the current character to pre
        minHeap.pop(); // Remove this character from the heap

        // Now we need to check if pre contains the lexicographically smallest character
        while (!pre.empty() && pre.back() <= minHeap.top()) {
            post += pre.back(); // Move the last character of pre to post
            pre.pop_back();     // Remove it from pre
        }
    }

    // After finishing the iteration, move the remaining pre characters to post
    while (!pre.empty()) {
        post += pre.back();
        pre.pop_back();
    }

    return post; // The lexicographically smallest string
}

int main() {
    string s = "eax";
    cout << "The lexicographically smallest string is: " << minimalString(s) << endl;
    return 0;
}

#include <stdlib.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <sys/types.h>

int main() {
    pid_t pid;
    pid = fork();

    if (pid < 0) {
        perror("");
        exit(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }
    else if (pid == 0) {
        printf("Child: I am the child process.\n");
        pid_t parent_pid = getppid();
        printf("Child: Yes, I am your child! Parent ID: %d\n", parent_pid);
  }
  else{
    printf("I am the parent process.\n");
    wait(NULL);
    printf("Parent:My child has responded");
    
  }

    return 0;
}

10/12/24, 11:43 - Satwik Geu: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <algorithm>

using namespace std;

long minimizeTotalIncrease(vector<int>& threadSize) {
    int n = threadSize.size();
    long totalIncrease = 0;

    // Iterate through the segments, excluding the first and last segments
    for (int i = 1; i < n - 1; i++) {
        if (!(threadSize[i - 1] < threadSize[i] && threadSize[i] > threadSize[i + 1])) {
            // Calculate the minimum increase needed to make this segment special
            int leftDiff = threadSize[i - 1] - threadSize[i] + 1;
            int rightDiff = threadSize[i + 1] - threadSize[i] + 1;

            int increase = max(leftDiff, rightDiff);
            if (increase > 0) {
                threadSize[i] += increase;
                totalIncrease += increase;
            }
        }
    }

    return totalIncrease;
}

int main() {
    // Input: number of segments
    int n;
    cin >> n;

    // Input: stack sizes of each segment
    vector<int> threadSize(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> threadSize[i];
    }

    // Compute the minimum total increase to maximize special segments
    long result = minimizeTotalIncrease(threadSize);

    // Output the result
    cout << result << endl;

    return 0;
}
